as of January 1, 2023, Kiora Pharmaceuticals, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) moved its corporate headquarters to 332 Encinitas Boulevard,
Suite 102, Encinitas, California 92024. The Company&#8217;s telephone number remains the same: </span>(781) 788-9043.</p>
